rgya gar skad du/ shrI sarba ta thA ga tagu h+ya tan+t+ra yo ga ma hA rA dzA dwa ya sa ma tA bi dza ya nA ma badzra shrI wa ra ma hA kalpA di/ bod skad du/ dpal de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba rnal 'byor chen po rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba mnyam pa nyid gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rdo rje dpal mchog chen po brtag pa dang po'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa yi// dus gcig tshe na bcom ldan 'das// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje// rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyi ni// b+ha ga la ni snyoms par zhugs// gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba// gsang ba chen po 'di lta ste// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi bdag // gsang ba pa rnams ma lus pa'i// sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje// byang chub sems kyi snying po che// chos kun mnyam pa nyid dgongs pa'i// mnyam nyid gnyis su med pa'i gnas// spyod pa mnyam pa zhes bya ba'i// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs te// de nyid ngang la gnas pa yis// 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dpag med la// gzigs shing mi phyed rdo rje las// ma g.yos lham me lhang nger gnas// mi 'gyur gsang ba 'dus pa'o// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // rig pa'i lha mo rdzu 'phrul can// sna tshogs 'khor rnams 'dus pa ste// rnal 'byor dbang phyug tshogs rnams las// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che// kun tu bzang pos gsol ba btab// rang gi stan las langs nas ni// bla gos phrag bar gzar gyur pas// pus mo sa la btsugs nas ni// thal mo sbyar te spyis btud nas// gsang ba zhes ni gang la bya// ches gsang ba ni ji lta bu// gsang ba chen po ji ltar lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis gsung du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// 'khor rnams kun la rjes brtse bas// rdo rje gsang ba kun bdag nyid// rdo rje'i gsung gis bka' stsal pa// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// chos kyi dbyings ni snang ba che// rang bzhin 'od gsal yongs su dag // nam mkha'i dbyings bzhin dri ma med// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yi// rgyu dang mi rgyu'i dngos bdag nyid// dkyil 'khor bsdus dang spros pa'i tshul// bskyed dang gnas dang sdud par mdzad// nyan thos rang rgyal la sogs las// gsang ba bya ba spyod pa ste// pha rol phyin pa'i mdo sde las// gsang ba rnal 'byor rgyud du grags// phyi nang gsang ba'i rim shes pas// gsang chen rnal 'byor bla med rgyud// thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa// stong pa snying rje dbyer med phyir// bde chen byang chub sems mchog gsang // de nyid dpal ldan 'dus pa ste// zab dang rgya che'i snying po nyid// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gsung thugs// gnyis med mnyam pa ro gcig pas// phyag rgya chen po'i gnas 'di ni// thun mong ma yin rgyal po che// dam tshig spyod pa'i gnas 'di yin// legs so legs so sems dpa' che// kun du bzang po legs par nyon// rgyud rnams kun du ma bshad cing // khyad par dngos grub 'byung ba'i gnas// rim pa bla na med pa'i chos// snying po khyod la bstan par bya// e ma'o sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// byang chub sems mchog bla na med// rang 'byung ye shes bde ba'i mchog // 'dod chags can gyi skyes bu rnams// rab tu gdul ba'i don ched du// gsang ba'i spyod pa mchog gi chos// gzhung nyung rtogs par sla ba'i don// 'dus pa chen po rdo rje'i tshig // rtogs dka' sangs rgyas spyod yul pas// sdom pa gsang ba rgyas gdab phyir// dri med ye shes 'byung gnas gter// lhan cig skyes pa'i ngo bo nyid// dpal ldan sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag // rdo rje 'chang ba chen po'i yul// thabs las ma lus sangs rgyas 'byung // 'di nyid gsang ba'i chos nyid can// sku yi gsang ba ma skyes pa// sems can lus dang snang ba khyab// gsung gi gsang ba ma 'gags pas// thams cad sgra dang dbyer mi phyed// thugs kyi gsang ba skye ba med// phyag rgya chen po lam gyi mchog // 'khor 'das chos dang ro gcig pas// sbas pa gsang ba mi shes rnams// lus dang ngag dang sems rnams ni// dri mas khebs pa'i rang bzhin gyis// 'gro ba lnga sogs dag tu 'khod// gsang ba'i yi ge'i don ma mthong // ka kha ga g+ha nga / tsa tsha dza dz+ha nya/ Ta Tha Da D+ha Na/ ta tha da d+ha na/ pa pha ba b+ha ma/ ya ra la wa/ sha Sha sa ha/ ji srid ya ra la ha'i bar// ka kha ga mtha' na dz+ha'i mtha'// da d+ha'i mtha' dang ma mthar bcas// de de rtsa ba'i yi ge gsum// thog mtha' gsang ba e dang ba~M// dus gsum rdo rje'i yi ge'i gnas// 'byung dang 'byung las g+hur sgrar bcas// 'dus pa 'di ni sbas pa'o// rnal 'byor rgyud tshul sna tshogs rnams// rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor nges pa yis// du ma nyid du dbang bskur bas// thabs dang shes rab spyod pa yi// ye shes 'bar ba'i phung po yin// thabs dang thabs las byung ba yi// khyad par rim pa gang gis ni// mdo don mngon par bsdus pa yin// a A/ i I/ u U/ r-i r-I/ l-i l-I/ e ai/ o au/ a~M aH/ a ni skye ba med pa'i tshul// shes rab pha rol phyin sbyor ba// dbyangs kyi yi ge tha ma'i bar// stong nyid nam mkha'i chos rnams kyis// bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mchog // snying po'i yan lag dag tu bshad// thub pa chen pos chos phung po// brgyad khri bzhi stong gsungs pa las// dpal ldan 'dus pa'i snod yin te// de bas 'di ni rgyud kyi rtsa// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gsung thugs// yon tan phrin las rdo rje sogs// rnam pa sna tshogs ston pa ni// snying po kun las 'di bsdus yin// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po gsang ba pa'i lam gyur pa// rdo rje'i gsung gis bka' stsal don// bsgrub bya sgrub byed don bshad gsol// ces gsol ba btab pas rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos ji lta bar mkhyen cing thugs su chud nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis chos thams cad kyi sgo la 'jug pa ngo bo nyid med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor 'dus pa de dag thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rang bzhin dag cing bdag med pa'i// chos kyi dbyings ni spros dang bral// sna tshogs sgyu ma'i cho 'phrul ni// rang 'byung dag par 'char ba yin// rnal 'byor rnams la dngos grub kyi// 'bras bu nyams snang 'dzin dbye ba yis// zhe sdang gti mug 'dod chags dang // yid bzhin nor bu'i dam tshig ste// rigs lngar gyur pa 'di dag gis// 'dod dang thar pa rab bsgrubs pas// dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur// gyur pas// mnyam par lta ba mthong ba rnams// ye shes mnyam par rnam par rgyal ba zhes gsungs so// kun du bzang po sems dpa' che// ji ltar mnyam par lta ba dang // gnyis su med pa'i chos dag ni// bdag 'dzin ro mnyam rdo rje yis// gsang chen gnyis med rgyal ba 'dir// gnas pa rtsa dang g.yo ba rlung // mi shigs thig le'i ngo bo nyid// rang lus rdo rje'i rang bzhin la// bde ba chen po'i ye shes kyis// byang chub sems kyi rang bzhin te// thabs kyi myu gu dag gis ni// ban+du ka ni rgyas pa bzhin// sbrang rtsi bdud rtsi'i gnas yin te// yon tan dri med de nyid kyi// me tog rgyas pa'i chu skyes pa'o// rgyal ba'i rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' sems chen po// mig gi skye mched sbyong mdzad cing // sa yi snying po de bzhin gshegs// sku yi rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' chen po ni// rna ba'i skye mched rnam dag pa// phyag na rdo rje mthu stobs can// thugs kyi rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' chen po ni// sna yi skye mched sbyong gyur pa'i// nam mkha'i snying po'i mchog gyur pa// ting 'dzin rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che// lce yi skye mched dag byed pa// 'jig rten dbang phyug bla na med// gsung gi rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' zhi ba che// yid kyi skye mched rnam dag cing // dag pa'i sems mchog 'jam dbyangs sku// nam mkha'i rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' theg pa che// lus kyi skye mched dag pa po// sgrib pa thams cad rnam sel mdzad// dam tshig rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal dbang po// 'gro ba'i sems rgyud sbyong mdzad pa// kun du bzang po ye shes rol// chos dbyings rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje gzugs ni yid du 'ong // snang stong kun du rol pa yis/ chos rnams sgyu ma'i cho 'phrul ston/ gzugs kyi lha mo phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i sgra ni yid du 'ong // sgra dang sgra min las grol ba// stong nyid rang sgra 'byung ba po// sgra yi lha mo phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i dri ni yid 'ong mchog // sangs rgyas thugs mchod bde ba che// log pa sad par byed pa po// dri yi lha mo phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje ro ni dga' ba'i sku// dri med bdud rtsi 'thob byed cing // dkyil 'khor ma lus mchod byed pa// ro yi lha mo phyag 'tshal lo// ya mAn+ta kr-ita sngags las skyes// sku yi gsang ba khro bo che// dbang po mnan cing shar phyogs bzhugs// gshin rje gshed la phyag 'tshal lo// pradz+nyAn+ta kr-ita sngags las skyes// thugs las skyes pa'i khro rgyal ni// gshin rje mnan cing lho phyogs bzhugs// rnam par rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo// pad+mAn+ta kr-ita sngags las skyes// gsung mchog pad+ma rang 'byung ba// chu bdag mnan cing nub phyogs bzhugs// gsung mchog rgyal la phyag 'tshal bstod// big+hanAn+ta kr-ita sngags las skyes// phrin las sna tshogs mdzad pa po// gnod sbyin mnan cing byang phyogs bzhugs// bdud rtsi 'khyil la phyag 'tshal bstod// rnam par rtog pas mi g.yo zhing // ye shes gsang ba'i don ldan pa'i// khro rgyal byin za'i steng bzhugs pa// mi g.yo mgon la phyag 'tshal lo// brtul zhugs chen po mi bzad pas// log 'dren dpung rnams 'joms mdzad pa// khro rgyal bden bral steng na bzhugs// 'dod pa'i rgyal po phyag 'tshal lo// gtum po srid gsum 'joms mdzad cing // snying rje'i stobs dang ldan pa'i sku// rlung bdag steng gnas khro bo che// dbyug sngon can la phyag 'tshal lo// dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi// ye shes mchog gis dbang bskur ba// khro rgyal dbang ldan steng bzhugs pa// stobs po che la phyag 'tshal lo// dug gsum rtog pa dag byas shing // sna tshogs sgyu mar gar mdzad pa// tshangs pa'i steng bzhugs lha yi gtso// 'khor los sgyur la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems kyi rang bzhin sku// spros med de bzhin nyid las byung // kA la kro d+ha gnon mdzad pa// khro rgyal gnod mdzes phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems las rang byung ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi de bzhin nyid// sgyu ma dag la spros med sku// 'od gsal bde ba'i bsam gtan nyid// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya las// rlung sngags las byung rang dag cing // thams cad chos ni yongs rdzogs par// snang ba ye shes rang bzhin tshogs// spro dang bsdu ba nyid gyur pa// zung 'jug ting 'dzin la 'jug gang // dbye bas ye shes dag pa'i gnas// mchod pas yang dag thob par 'gyur// de nyid bla ma'i sku nyid do// zhes gsungs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa dpal rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba'i rgyud las gsang ba chen po rab tu dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs dang yon tan dang phrin las kyi bkod pa du mar ston pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de bzhin gshegs pa du ma'i rigs kyi dkyil 'khor chen po gsang ba bla na med pa'i rdo rje mngon par rab tu ston pa/ rab 'byam chos kyi dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po tshad dang rgya yongs su chad pa med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas kyi zhing khams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs de nas bcom ldan 'das shin tu grags pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi khyu mchog rlabs po che'i rtsal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rang sems 'byung ba'i// bde chen rang 'byung rang nyid ni// mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lo ste// gsang ba'i tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rin chen grags pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnyis med mnyam pa rang byung rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gsang ba rang byung brtan g.yo bcas// thams cad rang nyid dkyil 'khor dang // bde chen zab pa'i tshul rdo rje// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das skyon rab zhi bas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes sgron me'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rtag tu dmigs par bcas pa yi// phyag rgya chen po dngos med de// dngos med ngo bo nyid du dag // rin chen tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das bdud rtsi 'chang bas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mig 'phrul ston pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa ni// stong nyid snying rje dbyer med pa// byang chub sems kyi ngo bor gcig // de nyid tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' che// kun du bzang pos slar gsol pa// dri med mnyam pa ye shes sku// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid de// gnas dang ston pa rang byung ba// che ba'i bdag nyid slad gnas pa// dpal mchog gsang ba 'di nyid du// skal ldan rgyal ba bla na med// ces gsungs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor rang byung du bstan pa'i bdag nyid rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba las le'u nyi shu pa'o// // de nas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs bcas dpag med dang // rnal 'byor dbang phyug byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs// rigs dang lha mor bcas pa dpag med dang // khro bo'i rgyal po du mar bcas pa dag // gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor gcig tu 'dus byas nas// bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gtso// byang chub sems kyi rdo rje'i bdag po la// tshogs pa 'dus pa brjod kyis mi lang ba'i// 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnams kyis dpag med ldan// mchod pa'i rim pa phyi nang gsang ba dang // de kho na nyid rnam pa mtha' yas pas// ye shes rgyal ba mi zad dam tshig gi// rin chen sprin gyis yang dag par mchod de// mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas ni 'di skad gsol// phyogs bcu dus gsum de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs// ma lus 'dus pa kun gyi gsang ba'i don// thog ma dbus mthar gnas pa ye shes che// gsang ba rdo rje snying po lhan cig skyes// brjod bya bla med gyur pas 'dus pa'i chos// snying po'i 'bras bu kun gyi rtsa ba gang // thabs dang bstan pa de yi khyad par mang // bcom ldan dri med gsang ba bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs// dpal ldan byang chub sems rdo rjes// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs rnams la// gsang ba byang chub bka' stsal to// phun sum tshogs pa'i 'khor rnams la// rab tu gzigs nas dgyes gyur pas// bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs pa rnams// gnas 'di zhus pa shin tu legs// legs so legs so sems dpa' che// zab cing rgya che mchog gi yul// 'on kyang 'dir ni bde gshegs kyang // the tshom 'jug pa'i gnas yin na// de las gzhan par gyur pa yi// byang chub sems dpar gyur pa'i tshogs// de las spyod yul lta ci smos// de nas bcom ldan 'das thams cad// mchog don ngo mtshar spyod pa dang // thun mong gnas la dmang gyur pa// zab pa dang ni rgya che la// the tshom thams cad gcod mdzad pa// dkyil 'khor sa yi bdag po la// 'di skad ces ni zhus par 'gyur// gnas dang dus dang phyag rgya dang // 'dus pa khyad par gyur pa la'ang // gsang ba dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du// tshad med ye shes zhing khams kyi// snang ba rab tu rgyas pa la// rgyu thabs khyad par gyur pa yi// gsang chen sku gsung thugs kyi gsang // de nyid 'dus pa 'di mchog tu// ston pa 'phro bar ma gyur pa// de srid du ni kun mkhyen gyis// lhan cig skyes pa'i 'dus pa las// lus ngag yid ni byin brlab cing // khyad par mchog dbang bskur mdzad de// phyi nang gsang ba'i rim phye ba// bum pa dang ni gsang ba dang // shes rab ye shes de bzhin du// rab tu bskur bas smin byas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ gsang ba byang chub sems rdo rje// rtogs dka' mi phyed dam tshig gis// gang phyir dgongs te bshad pa dang // dgongs min drang ba'i don gyur dang // nges don ji bzhin pa dang ni// ji bzhin ma yin rnam phye bas// yi ge'i don dang spyi yi don// sbas pa gsum dang mthar thug gnyis// dang po gcig dang tshul gnyis ldan// dpag med rdo rje'i tshig gi rgya// nges phyir rab tu ston pa nyid// 'jug bya de dag lus ngag yid// rim pa gnyis kyi bde ba dang // yid bde rab tu myong bgyid pa// thabs zab rgya che myur ba'i lam// yan lag dam tshig ldan pa yi// thob bya thob byed khyad par pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// mkhyen pa'i ye shes bla med pa// mngon pa'i ye shes bla na med// mngon par byang chub gnas gyur pa'i// 'bras bu yang dag thob gyur nas// gsang ba'i rgyud mchog bstan du gsol// de ltar gsol ba btab gyur pas// de nas bla med bcom ldan 'das// de bzhin gshegs kun gtso bo yis// gsang ba byang chub sems rdo rje// de bzhin gshegs pa du ma rnams// stong pa nyid du 'jug pa yi// dpag med zil gnon rdo rje zhes// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs// de nas gsang ba'i bdag po de// 'od gsal dri med dbyings nyid la// ye shes 'jug pa'i ngo bo yis// dbyer med gnas par gyur ma thag // rdo rje'i lus kyi rtsa gnas ni// stong phrag bdun cu la sogs pa// rtsa yi bu ga khong stong dag // thig le zhu ba'i gzugs kyis ni// byang chub rdo rje'i rnam par ni// zhu zhing yang dag gnas par gyur// de nyid chos sku'i ngo bo nyid// bde dang stong pa dbyer med pa/ snying rje tshad med rnam pa las/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje/ rnam pa rang ben don nyid du gnas// sgyu ma sbyong ba'i dam tshig dang / mngon par byang chub 'od gsal ba'i// stong nyid rdo rje rdzogs pa yi// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs nas// rig pa thabs dang shes rab dag // dbyer med bde ba chen po'i sku// skyes bu'i rnam par gyur pa dag // gnas pa'i ngang las ldang ba ste// phung po khams dang skye mched dang // yul dang dngos po rnam dag pa'i// sku gsung thugs ni byin brlabs pa// ye shes chen po'i ngang gnas pa// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa// ston ka'i 'dam bu'i mdog 'dra ba// sprin dkar dag pa'i tshul can nyid// de ma thag tu snang bar mdzad// byin gyis brlabs pa'i rjes zhugs pa// mtshan dang dpe byad 'bar ba dang // rang 'byung ye shes lhag pa'i lha// thams cad bdag po rdo rje 'dzin// zhal gsum pa la phyag drug pa// sna tshogs rin chen gyis brgyan cing // in dra ni la 'bar ba dang // dang po mgon po rnam par sprul// dung dang kun da ltar dkar ba// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// dkyil 'khor gnas pa'i rang bzhin gyis// rnam pa gsal ba nyid du gzigs// de nas sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin// rnam par snang mdzad chen po nyid// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// 'dod chags kyis 'dul 'gro gzigs nas// 'dod chags gsang ba'i tshul zhes pa'i// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi// bkod pa rab tu mi zad pa// de dag thams cad bsdus nas ni// nyid kyi sku la thim par mdzad// de nas 'dus pa'i lha tshogs kyis// dbyer med gnas pa'i dad las ni// rdo rje 'dzin pa gsang ba'i bdag // yongs su mnyes pa'i don du ni// nyid kyi sku las spros pa yi// ba spu'i bu ga'i 'od zer gyi// rtse mo rnams las spros gyur pa// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad du// sangs rgyas spyan dang mA ma kI// gos dkar mo dang sgrol ma dang // gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro// reg bya rdo rjer gyur pa yis// sa dang chu dang me dang rlung // tshad med yul dang spyod pa yis// chags pa chen pos rjes chags nas// bde ba'i rol pa ston par mdzad// rnam par snang mdzad ye shes che// de nyid me long sogs bdag nyid// gsang ba 'dzin pa thub pa'i rgyal// rdo rje mi bskyod rgyal po nyid// gsang ba 'dzin pa ma lus pa'i// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyal// snying po rdo rje ye shes so// de nyid rdo rje btsun mo rnams// gcig tu gyur pa'i mkha' dbyings ni// dam tshig chen po'i mkha' dbyings te// rnyog pa med cing rdul med pa'i// dkyil 'khor gru bzhir byin brlabs pa// phyogs mtshams mnyam par ldan pa la// grub pa'i gnas brgyad yongs bskor ba// zhing khams yongs su dag pa yi// 'dzam gling pad ma'i lte ba la// sna tshogs mi shigs e dang ba~M// gsal ba de yi ngo bo nyid// sna tshogs gzugs kyi kun du rgyas// sangs rgyas sprin gyis kun du khyab// 'od zer 'phro ba mang po 'khrug // gsal ba la sogs dkyil 'khor ldan// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// de nas sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag // gsang ba rab tu 'dzin pa po// dkyil 'khor nyi shu rtsa lnga pa// sum cu gsum par ldan pa yis// pho brang yangs pa'i gzhal yas der// de bzhin gshegs pa stong dang ni// gnyis dang byang chub sems dpar bcas// phyi rol 'jig rten skyong ba bzhi// sna tshogs dkyil 'khor chen po yi// dbus su yang dag bzhugs gyur pa'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs// mi bskyod pa dang dkon mchog dpal// tshe dpag med dang gdon mi za// dpal ldan rnam par snang mdzad sogs// de bzhin gshegs pa thub pa'i rgyal// de nyid sku gsung thugs ye shes// phrin las ldan par bzhugs pa'o// de nas rang bzhin dag pa yi// chos kyi dbyings na gnas gyur pa// dbyings dang ye shes dbyer med pa'i// sems can khams kyi snod bcud dang // yul dang dbang po thams cad kun// rdo rje sems dpas byin brlabs shing // dbang bskur sngags dang phyag rgya dang // ye shes kyi ni dbang bsgyur bas// de dag thob pa'i khyad par ni// tha ma 'bring dang mchog rnams la// bde ba dang ni yid bde bas// gsang ba ye shes spyod yul thob// de las sprul pa'i sku byung ba// bcom ldan de nyid thugs ka nas// sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor dpag med pa// bye ba grangs med bkye nas ni// gdul bya gdul phyir dbang bskur zhing // spyi dang khyad par gyis 'dul 'gyur// de nas sangs rgyas tshogs dag gis// bskul bas ched du brjod pa gsungs// e ma ho sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // byang chub sems ni rang byung ba// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis// rab tu rtog med mi gnas pa'o// de nas bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs// sku bzhi ye shes ro gcig pas// mdzad pa thams cad rdzogs byed pa// rab 'byam cho 'phrul ston pa'o// dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo nges par sprul pas rgyud nges par bstan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// phyi rol yul snang rdzas su 'dod// g.yag rnga ne'u gsing lta bu la// bar du snang mun shong ba tsam// sems las tha dad par gnas pa// skad cig mi rtag par 'dod pas// yul sems tha dad bye brag smra// phyi rol yul dag phra ba rnams// 'dus nas rigs pa 'byung ba ltar/ yul dus rnam par nges pa las// rigs pa 'dra ba'i rnam par bzhag // yul dgag pa yi tha ma dang // shes pa skye ba'i thog ma ru// phrad par 'dod pa grub pa'i mtha'// mdo sde pa yi dgongs pa smra// chos rnams thams cad rang gi sems// rnam par rig tsam skad cig ma// rang gsal rgyun gnas spros bral 'dod// rang rig skad cig gsal ba dang // mi gsal sna tshogs rtog bral du// rnam med rnal 'byor spyod pa smra// dngos rnams stong pa sgyu ma bzhin// snang yang bdag las rang stong pa// sems kyi rtog pa rnam bzlog ste// mkha' dbyings dri med rtog rgyun 'chad// 'di ltar srid pa zhi ba las// rnam grol stong nyid snying rje dang // dbyer med byang chub sems kyi mchog // zung 'jug rab tu mi gnas pa// dpal ldan 'dus 'dir grub mtha' kun// blo yi rim pas 'dir 'dus te// de bas 'dir ni chos kun gyi// snying po 'dus pa'i rtsa bar gsungs// gsang ba bla na med pa'i don// ye shes rnam gsum rim 'jug cing // sgron me 'od gsal snang ba las// zung 'jug rdo rje mi phyed pa// lha yi 'khor lo sprul nas ni// dbyer med mi g.yo ting nge 'dzin// mchog ni dri med rang snang las// gnyis med ngang du rab zhugs pa'o// byang chub sems kyi ngang nyid las// rtag tu 'od gsal bar gnas kyang // 'gro ba'i don las mi 'da' bas// dam tshig 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin// byang chub sems kyi za ma tog // bde ba can ni mi shigs pa// rin chen 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin// bde ba chen po'i byang chub sems// 'gro ba kun la ster ba ni// ma chags pa yi ye shes kyis// 'dod chags 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin// rnam pa sna tshogs sgyu ma las// gdon mi za ba gnas med pa// 'od gsal 'bras bu mngon phyogs pa// dam tshig 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin// zag pa med pa'i dga' ba yis// ye shes chen po'i ros khyab pas// rdo rje 'dzin pa mnyes gyur pa'i// dam tshig bla med ting nge 'dzin// yang dag ye shes nor bu ltar// rin chen 'od 'phro sprin tshogs kyis// sangs rgyas thams cad rjes su yang // mnyes byed rdo rje ting nge 'dzin// zag pa bsdus byas bde ba las// bcu drug 'gyur gyis khyad 'phags pa// 'dod chags rjes su 'dzin byed pa// chags par byed pa'i ting nge 'dzin// sku gsung thugs nyid rdo rje las// mi phyed 'od gsal bar thim la// sgyu ma slu ba rdo rje nyid// snang ba thim pas ting nge 'dzin// ye shes me long lta bu las// srid gsum snang bar mdzad pa ste// snang mdzad rdo rje 'khor lo ni// mi zad sku yi ting nge 'dzin// snang ba gsum las 'das pa yi// rang bzhin mngon par byang chub pa// rnam par dag pa rdo rje yi// 'od gsal ba yi ting nge 'dzin// srid zhi mnyam nyid mnyam pa'i sku// chos rnams gnyis med ro gcig pas// rin po che ltar 'byung ba'i gnas// yon tan gter gyur ting nge 'dzin// phyogs bcu dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi// gang las 'od gsal chos kyi sku// mngon par byang chub pa yi tshul/ mi phyed rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin/ bla med mngon par byang chub pa// gsang ba lhan cig skyes pa yi// ye shes rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin// rtogs pa'i ye shes mchog tu 'gyur// chos nyid mi zad dbyings kyi dang // snang stong tha dad med pa ste// ro gcig 'du 'bral med pa nyid// stong dang snying rje'i ting nge 'dzin// chos rnams thams cad bdag med pas// kun du stong zhing ma bcos pa// lhun grub rdo rje'i ngang gnas pa// phyag rgya chen po'i ting nge 'dzin// rnam par mi rtog ye shes kyi// 'od chen rnam par snang bar byed// 'od gsal 'bar ba rdo rje yis// tshe dpag med pa'i ting nge 'dzin// snang ba'i dngos po sna tshogs pa// sgyu ma rkyen skyes zil gnon pa// rdo rje 'od gsal ting nge 'dzin// dmigs pa med pa'i snying rje can// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag rab tu dga' bas khyab cing dgyes pa chen po yongs su spyod par 'gyur ro// de nas gsang ba gsum gyi dngos// rdo rje 'dzin pas 'di gsungs so// dka' thub sdom pa mi zad pas// lus skams gyur cing sdug bsngal gyur// sdug bsngal gyi ni sems byings te// de la dngos grub gzhan du gyur// brjod pa thams cad yi ge ste// kun gyi rtsa ba a las byung // de las chos kyi phung po ni// brgyad khri bzhi stong dag tu snang // dbyangs dang gsal byed ngag yin te// ngag ni rlung gi rtsa ba can// sgrar snang tsam nyid kun rdzob ste// thim pa don dam brjod pa'o// yang gnas 'di la sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin ni 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga'i yul la rang gi bsod nams dang ye shes gnyis su med par spyad pa spyod par byed de/ rang rig pa'i ye shes sgyu ma dang mtshungs pas spyad pa spyod par byed do// 'di ltar chos rnams thams cad gzugs brnyan dang / sprul pa dang / sgra brnyan dang / brag ca dang / dri za'i grong khyer dang / chu zla dang / smig rgyu dang / rmi lam dang / dbang po'i gzhu dang / sprin dang / mig yor dang / glog dang / chu'i chu bur dang / sgyu ma'i rnam par blta ste/ de lta na yang don dam pa ni rnam par dmigs su med do// chos thams cad ni rang bzhin med pa'i phyir rten 'brel tshogs pa'i snang ba dgag tu med do// de yang dag par bden pas stong pa'i phyir ro// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs 'dus pa rnams kyis mngon par dga' ba'i yid kyis dpal rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po la legs so legs so// gsang ba'i gnas kyi spyod pa ngo mtshar zhing rmad du rab tu byung ba rab tu bstan pa gsang ba'i spyod yul la dgongs te rang rang gi stan la gnas par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa rnam par rgyal ba'i rgyud las dman pa'i spyod pa las ring zhing lam bde ba chen pos ye shes la rol pa bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o// // rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi gsang // gsang ba gsum du gnas pa gang // byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngor// gsang ba rab tu gyur pa gsungs// gsang ba'i yi ge rtogs dka' ba// ma 'ongs skye bo gdul slad du// dkyil 'khor lha rnams thams cad kyi// phyi nang sbas pa rim pas bstan// e yi rnam pas lha mo spyan// ba~M gi rnam pa bdag mar brjod/ ma ni lha mo gos dkar mo// yA ni rnam pa sgrol mar brjod// shru ni byang chub sems rdo rje// ta~M ni shes rab pha rol phyin// me long ye shes e zhes brjod// ka ni mi bskyod rdo rje ste// smin zhes don yon grub pa nyid// rin chen 'byung ba sa zhes bya// 'od dpag med pa ma zhes brjod// rtag pa'i rdo rje ye zhes pa'o// b+ha ni dri yi rdo rje ma'o// yi ge ga ni ro rdo rje// bAn ni gzugs kyi rdo rje ma'o// sa yi rnam pa reg rdo rje// rba ni sgra yi rdo rje ma// ta ni chos dbyings rdo rje yi// thA ni sgrib pa rnam par sel// ga ni 'jig rten dbang phyug brjod// yi ge ta ni sa snying po'o// kA ni nam mkha'i snying po ste// ya ni phyag na rdo rjer gnas// bAka ni kun du bzang po'o// tsita ni byams par brjod par bya// ta ni 'dod pa'i rgyal po ste// hr-i da ya ni snying po nyid// ba ni dbyug sngon can du grags// dzra ni stobs chen 'bar ba ste// yo ni mi g.yo gtum po'o// Shid ni bya ba nan tan te// b+ha ni gnod mdzes rgyal po'o// ge ni gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur// Shu ni bgegs mthar byed pa ste// pi ni shes rab mthar byed do// dza ni gshin rje mthar byed de// ha ni mthar byed pad ma 'dzin// ra ni so sor rtog pa nyid// thabs dang shes rab mnyam sbyor ba// phung po lnga ni sangs rgyas lnga// 'byung bzhi lha mo bzhi ru brjod// yul lnga 'dod yon lha mo lnga// rnam shes brgyad ni byang chub sems// lus tshigs la gnas khro rgyal bcu// bsdus pa ye shes lngar sbyor ba// bde ba chen po'i ye shes ni// dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang gi dngos// mig dang mi yis gnas pa las// de nyid kyis ni sbyar ba yis// de las gyur pa'i grangs rnams kyi// dkyil 'khor de snyed rnams su 'gyur// phyogs dang gdengs ka gdong ba dang // ris byed rigs kyis phye ba gang // rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor gyur pa ste// gzhan du 'phros pa'i dkyil 'khor yin// ka nas bzung ste rim bzhin du// de bzhin ha yi bar dag tu// de dag sna tshogs rgyur gyur pa// stong phrag sum cu'i bdag nyid do// thabs dang shes rab ngo bo nyid// stong phrag sum cu rtsa bzhir 'gyur// rtsa ba'i rgyud dang bshad pa dang // cha mthun yan lag rgyud gyur pas// de dag sde dang bcas pa yis// gsang chen rgyud sder brjod par bya// rnal 'byor rgyud ni thams cad du// lha 'di rnams ni thog mar bzhugs// 'dis ni rgyud rnams gsang chen kun// rnal 'byor rgyud ces rgyas btab pa'o// mdo sde rnams la gnas sogs pa// thun mong dbye bas phye ba nyid// yi ge bzhi ni thun mong du// bsdus pas chos kyi bdag nyid can// mdo kun yul du gyur pa'o// gsang ba'i gnas kyi mtshan nyid ni// nyan thos rang rgyal la sogs pas// rnam pa kun du ma bshad de// 'di skad bdag ces dang por brjod// dus gcig dus gsum skad cig ste// ston pa rang 'byung che ba'i sku// de bzhin gshegs pa bde bar gshegs// de bzhin du ni rtag gshegs la// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje zhes// pad+ma'i ming can btsun mo'i gnas// der ni mngon par bzhugs par mdzad// btsun mo rdo rje sems dpa' dang // rin chen chos dang bcas pa yi// rdo rje las kyi sems mar brjod// de dag kun gyi bde ba'i gnas// bskyed dang sdud par mdzad pa po// thams cad nam mkha'i mtshan nyid can// phung po khams dang skye mched dang // yul rnams thams cad rten pa'i gzhi// yang dag btsun mo'i b+ha ga der// phyogs bcu dus gsum sangs rgyas rnams// mngon par rab tu zhugs mdzad de// spro dang bsdu ba'i ngo bo nyid// rab tu mi gnas dbyer med bzhugs// mdo dang gsang bar spyod pa'i tshul// don gcig na yang ma rmongs dang // thabs mang dka' ba med pa dang // dbang po rnon po'i dbang byas phyir// gsang sngags theg pa khyad par 'phags// gsang ba bya ba spyod pa'i rgyud// shin tu ches gsang rnal 'byor rgyud// rnal 'byor bla med gsang chen no// 'di ni sku gsung thugs gsang ba// mtshan dang dpe byad rnams dang ni// rjod byed rang gi mtshan nyid de// phung po khams dang skye mched sogs// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor la zhugs pa// rten dang brten par bcas pa ni// mkhas pa rnams la bsngags pa yin// rmongs pa de ltar 'dod pa rnams// skye dang 'jig dang gnas pa dang // rgyud gzhan rnams la nges bstan pa// rtag tu rten 'brel tshul de brjod// 'bras bu rgyus ni rgyas btab cing // rgyu la 'bras bus rgyas gdab par// bsam gyi gzhar du dngos grub ni// bskal pa bye bar yang mi 'gyur// rgyud kun la ni gsang chen gyi// snying po phyag rgyas rgyas gdab phyir// de nyid gsang ba yang dag par// mi phyed par ni bstan pa yin// sems can kun gyi lus gnas pa// sku yi gsang ba rtag pa nyid// sems can kun gyi ngag la ni// gsung gi gsang ba rang byung du// sems can kun gyi snying la ni// thugs kyi gsang ba snying po bzhugs// de nyid snying po gsum ldan pa// bde gshegs snying po 'jug pa nyid// sems can sangs rgyas sgras btags so// sku yi dngos grub snang ba'i dngos// mi zad sprul pas 'gro don spyod// gsung gi dngos grub brag ca ltar// brjod pa du ma'i sgra ru ston// thugs kyi dngos grub rtog pa'i tshogs// ye shes bde chen bsam mi khyab// ting 'dzin sems kyi spyod pa ni// stong nyid ye shes dngos grub bo// de nyid byang chub sems rdo rje// bla ma nyid du bsdus pa yin// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug gsum// 'dzin pas dug tu 'gyur ba yin// dug nyid nye bar zhi gyur na// dag pas dug med byas pa yin// bdud rtsi rim gyis bsten na ni// bdud rtsi nyid du nges 'gyur yin// de nyid ngo bo yongs shes pas// rgyud 'dir lam du gyur pa yin// sngags 'dun thabs dang shes rab ste// dbyer med de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs// shes rab b+ha ga'i brdar brtags pas// dbyangs su brjod pa gsang ba'i tshul// A li bcu gnyis rten 'brel te// ma rig la sogs 'gag par bstan// ro hi ta la sogs pa dang // khyim ni bcu gnyis rlung dag ste// dus sbyor ba dang mtshungs pas na// lugs 'byung de nyid lugs bzlog par// de nyid yang dag rim pas bstan// kA li sum cu rtsa bzhi po// thabs kyi yi ge pha zhes brjod// mi gtsang rdzas ni sum cu bzhi// dag pa byang sems rang bzhin te// khams ni rang bzhin gyis dag pa'i// de dag dag pas ye shes che// dag pa'i dus ni dpe byad dag // nyis 'gyur dag gis bstan pa ste// thabs dang shes rab phrag gnyis bstan// A li shes rab ma ning bcas// 'di dag mtshan mchog sum cu gnyis// cha gnyis rab tu dbye ba yis// sems can kun gyi lus gnas pa// kla zhes bya ba chu yin te// sla zhes bya bas yin no// l+la zhes bya ba me yin te// sh+la zhes bya ba rlung yin te// 'byung bzhi'i dbye ba ma ning ste// ye shes dag pa chen po nyid// yang dag lam gsal phyogs tsam dang // mi gsal ba nyid rgyud las 'byung // rkyen nyid tshogs gnyis rdzogs byed pa// bsod nams bla med 'bras bur 'gyur// gzhi ni khong na gnas pa'i don// sems can kun gyi lus la gnas// de yod pas na 'gro kun kyang // ye shes snying po can gyur pas// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyu ru bshad// ma ning ye shes dag pa nyid/ gnyis med ye shes 'bar ba yi// A li snang ba thabs kyi cha// mched pa ka sogs shes rab cha// ma ning thob pa gnyis med pa'o// sbyor ba don gyi yi ge bzhi// sbas pa'i tshul du bstan pa'o// char ni stong pa tsheg drag dang // thig les brgyan pa bde ba che// dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' la// kun du bzang po sems dpa' ches// gsang ba zab dang rgya che ba'o// lhag pa'i gsang chen rgyud kyi don// byang chub sems dpa' grags chen rnams// khyad par nges shes bskyed don du// dpal ldan 'dus pa nges gsal ba'i// bla med dgongs rgyud bshad du gsol// de nas gsang ba 'dzin pa po// rdo rje 'chang ba tshul 'di dag // rnal 'byor rgyud kyi sbas pa'i don// gsang ba rin chen snying po gsungs// gsang chen gleng gzhi'i khyad par dang // rim pa gleng slong gyur pa dang // gsang bar bya ba'i gzhi gang dang // gsang ba'i dam tshig nges pa dang // gsang ba bsgrub pa'i cho ga dang // 'jug pa'i rnal 'byor ji ltar bstan// gsang chen rnam bshad thabs dang ni// de nyid dang 'brel brjod bya gang // rjod byed thun mong bstan pa'i tshul// lam la 'jug pa'i dbye ba dang // gsang ba grub pa'i 'bras bu dang // gsang ba lhag pa'i lam dang ni// gsang ba mchog gi spyod pa dang // gsang chen rnam par bsdu ba'i don// mi 'gyur rkyen gyis ldog bya dang // dgag sgrub gsang chen 'byung ba'i tshul// phyogs dang thub pa'i rnam dbye ba'i// gsang ba 'di dag gnas zhes bya// 'di nyid 'jug pa'i tshul shes nas// grub pa sgrub pa'i tshul spyod do// gsang ba rnam par dag pa ye shes kyi ting nge 'dzin bstan pa zhes bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// dang po'i mgon po bcom ldan 'das// dpal mchog gsang ba 'dzin pa yis// 'dus pa'i 'khor la bka' stsal 'gyur// gsum pa rab tu gsal ba yi// 'gro ba'i snang ba ye shes sgron// bzhi pa ye shes 'od 'phro ba// nyi ma'i snying po ltar 'char ba'o// lnga pa zla ba'i dkyil 'khor ltar// 'dzag dang smin cing sdud pas sbyor// drug pa sgyu ma'i gzugs brnyan ltar// chos rnams rang bzhin shes pa'o// bdun pa lta ngan phyogs las ni// rgyal 'gyur seng ge'i rgyal po bzhin// ri bo mchog ltar ting 'dzin rgyal// ji srid rlung ni mi rgyu dang // snang ba mi g.yo bar gyur pas// bdag gi dngos por rab tu brtag // thabs ldan byang chub sems mchog gis// don mdzad 'khor los sgyur ba'i stobs// legs thob phyir mi ldog pa'i thams cad kyang // snang ba gsum gyi rgyun chad dngos// ma lus yul la zhugs nas ni// de nyid du ni rang thim 'gyur// snang ba gsum po dag pa'i lam// rin chen sprin gyis 'gro don du// bsam pa'i tshul gyis char pa 'bebs// 'dod chags rnam par dag pa'i dngos// de nyid byang chub sems dpa'i yul// 'di ltar zhe sdang rnam par dag // de nyid byang chub sems dpa'i gnas// gang du gti mug dag pa'i ngang // dbyings// rin chen 'od 'phro mi zad dang // byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa sra ba'i dbang phyug sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rol pa ston pa'i dpal rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kun nas 'od kyi phreng ba dam pa'i dkyil 'khor 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor thams cad sems su gcig // de nyid ye shes dag pa'i ngang // dbyer med rtag pa'i tshul mchog ste// bde gshegs gsang ba 'byung ba'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa me tog spyan yangs sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mnga' dbang dam pa rnam par 'phrul ba dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rgyal ba kun gyi ye shes dbyings// gsang ba 'gro snying rnam dag pas// blang dor med pa'i bde ba thob// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par dbyes pa'i sku'i dpal sangs rgyas nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dkon pa'i tog rang 'byung du 'char ba'i ye shes rol ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'di ni rang 'byung ston pa po// ye shes 'jug pa 'bad med par// thob bya byang chub sems dpa' rnams// rang rig rang las rnyed par 'gyur// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa bla ma phan par grags pa sangs bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje sde sangs rgyas thams cad kyi tshul zla ba'i snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du rmi lam dag par ni// rdo rje blo yis rnam par sbyang // de nyid ye shes rgyal ba yis// bdud las rnam par rgyal bar bya// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje phal cher sbyin sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba pad+mo rnam par rol pa'i 'od zer 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// zhing khams kun gyi snang ba'i gnas// rin chen 'od kyis rnam par spras// sgyu ma tsam du ston pa nyid// snying po ye shes gzhir gyur pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zhi ba'i blo gros sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhing ma lus par bkod pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rgyal ba rgya mtsho sprin tshogs las// dus gsum kun tu dge ba yi// zhing khams ye shes 'od kyi sku// chos rnams sems kyi snang las 'byung // zhes gsungs so// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// gsang ba'i dbang phyug bcom ldan gyis// ye shes spyod pas bsgrub pa yi// lhan cig spyod pa bka' stsal to// ji ltar mi gnas nam mkha' ni// khyab cing mtshan nyid med pa nyid// don dam de nyid dmigs med de// brjod pa spangs pa stong pa che// mi shigs gsang ba bla na med// kun du bzang po zhes grags pa// rnal 'byor dbang phyug phyag rgya che// ye shes rtag pas chos kyi sku// me long nang gi gzugs brnyan gang // rnam pa gsal bar 'char ba ltar// ji ltar sangs rgyas ye shes ni// snang ba me long lta bur brjod// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// ye shes rang rig gzhan rig pa// tha dad med par thugs chud pas// de nyid mnyam nyid ye shes brjod// gdod nas dag cing skye ba med// rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal ba// phan tshun khyab pa'i ye shes la// so sor rtog pa zhes brjod do// kun nas ma lus sangs rgyas kyi// mdzad pa sna tshogs la spyod pas// bde bar gshegs gnas gcig mdzad pas// khyab pa nan tan ye shes brjod// gang tshe nyon mongs shes bya'i sgrib// thams cad las grol de yi tshe// rnal 'byor mchog thob rdo rje 'dzin// shin tu rnam dag ye shes brjod// mchog gyur rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas ni// chos rnams ngo bo nyid med pas// rab tu mi gnas ye shes gzhi// dam tshig shin tu 'da' dka' ba'o// rang byung dri ma med pa ni// rtog pa thams cad yang dag spangs// dngos dang dngos med rang bzhin gyis// gnyis kyi bag chags 'ching ba nyid// mi rtog pa yi rang bzhin gyis// bsam mi khyab pa nyid kyis gcod// rtog pa'i dri ma'i dra ba yis// rin chen sems ni dri mar byas// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes nyid// dri ma bral phyir sangs rgyas brjod// ces byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po la sogs pa rnams kyis gsang chen gyi gnas yongs su brjod pa la rab tu dga' ba'i don ched du brjod do// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba las sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes mngon par rol pa bstan pa'i le'u ste nyer lnga pa'o// // de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// thams cad stong pa mi 'gyur che// ye shes dam pa ston pa pos// kun du gsang ba bka' stsal to// dam chos snying po bcud las byung // sangs rgyas mchod pa bla med pa// byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul// shes rab thabs ni tshul thob byed// ji ltar gdul bya'i chos rnams dang // 'dod yon kun la sangs rgyas rnams// thams cad longs spyod tshul gcig pas// longs spyod rdzogs sku zhes bshad do// mtshan rnams kun dang yang dag ldan// sna tshogs sku ste mtshan nyid med// sangs rgyas rnams kyis sprul pas na// sprul pa'i sku zhes 'dir bshad yin// phyag rgya chen po rab bsgrub phyir// shes nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug sgom// kun rtog thams cad rnam spangs pas// rgyal ba chos sku ye shes nyid// bla ma'i byin brlabs skad cig gis// ye shes mi zad rgya mtsho ni// tshe 'di nyid la 'grub par 'gyur// mi phyed rdo rje dbang phyug nyid// gnyis med mnyam par ro gcig pas// rdo rje 'chang chen rang byung du// grub pa bde chen ngo bo nyid// thob med thob pas cig car grol// spangs thob med pa mnyam nyid che// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa spos kyi glang po'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi gnas 'byung ba rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zab pa'i rdo rje ye shes sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'dir ni chos rnams thams cad kyi// snying po ye shes bde chen po// byang chub rten cing 'brel 'byung ba'i// gsang ba'i tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa stobs mi zad pa sred med kyi bu sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dbyangs kun du bskul ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// bdag med dngos po med pa ru// ma skyes zag pa med pa'i ngang // spros pa kun las rnam grol ba'i// ye shes tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'gro ba skyob dbul po nges pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi glang po'i rtsal thogs pa med pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'byung gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rdo rje sems dpa' rang nyid de// rang sems zla ba kun+da ltar// sa bon gnas te rgyu yi cha// gsang ba'i tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi tshugs pa ye shes mtshungs pa med pa'i 'od sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zab pa'i mdzod rdo rje dbyings zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sangs rgyas kun gyi rdo rje'i thugs// rab tu mi gnas brjod med pa// byang chub sems su gcig pas na// thams cad dbyer med dag par brjod// ces gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa nyi zla sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rin po che'i nor bu'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dngos po kun gyi bdag nyid gang // stong gsum 'jig rten rang gi lus// phyi nang gnyis med ye shes che// gsang ba zab pa'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad tog gi 'od zer sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po 'od zer kun nas 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'gro ba skyob pa'i don du ni// sna tshogs gzugs can cho 'phrul gyis// gdul bya ye shes lam la bkod// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mchog gi mchod pa'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes mkha' lding rol pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du byams pa'i 'od kyis ni// 'gro ba kun la khyab par bya// des ni dpag med gzhan don du// mtshungs med ye shes gnas thob pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dpal gyi snying po sbas pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bdud thams cad rnam par 'jig par mdzad pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// byams pas bdud dpung 'joms mdzad cing // snying rje g.yul las rgyal bar 'gyur// byang chub sems kyis phyir mi ldog // ye shes tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes tog sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba ye shes rdo rje'i stobs zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rin chen 'bar ba glog gi 'od// dri med chu shel zer 'bab pas// tha mal lus ni rgyal bar bsgyur// de nyid tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes don grub sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mdzad pa rigs sna tshogs su ston pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du lha mo bye ba dang // byang chub sems dpa' khrag khrig tshogs// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs brgya dang // bde gshegs stong sogs tshul 'dir bstan// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ri rab lhun po brtsegs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi snying po sgyu ma'i rol pa ston pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du rgyu dang 'bras bu'i chos// ngo bo nyid dag rang byung ba// bdag med ye shes gnas med pa// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gdul dka' 'dul ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas la spyod pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// mchog tu sa yi mthar thug pa// bcu gsum ye shes rdo rje 'dzin// bde ba'i 'byung gnas bla na med// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das pad+mo'i 'od zer rnam par rol pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas mi zad pa 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du mnyam nyid ye shes dang // 'gro ba'i bla ma chos don gyis// tshad med thugs rjes yongs su bsdu// de nyid mi rtog gsang ba'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom grags pa'i 'od zer sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kun nas chos kyi sgra 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du sdud cing spro ba dang // mtshan bcas dmigs pa med pa ru// ye shes rgyal la phyag rgyas btab// 'di ni dag pa'i don ston pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes grogs rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba nges par rtogs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sangs rgyas kun gyis nam mkha'i khams// yongs su gang ba til 'bru bzhin// sems can smin cing grol byed pas// ye shes mngon par bsdus pa yin// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes nyon mongs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'phro ba'i sprin bkod pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du dngos dang dngos med pas// mi phyed ye shes bde ba che// sna tshogs 'du 'bral med pa'i ngang // ye shes phyag rgya chen por bstan// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'dam bu'i 'od sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// nam mkha'i khams kyi spyod yul bas// rang bzhin gyis ni mi dmigs bzhin// don dam thob tu med pa'i don// gzhi med tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa spos bzang rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po'i 'od zer kun nas rgyas pas lta ngan skrag par byed pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// mtshan nyid dang ni mtshan gzhi med// gang du ro mnyam zung 'jug pas// dbyer med rtogs pa rgyal po che// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa yul 'khor rangs pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gshegs pa dang byon pa rjes su 'gro ba ston pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// mi g.yo 'gyur ba med pa las// de bzhin nyid du bstan pa yis// 'jug cing 'byung ba gsang ba che// snying po ye shes tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa bde grags dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dngos grub gnas pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dngos grub snying po bdud rtsi'i bcud// grub pa'i bla ma'i gdams pa las// thob 'gyur de bas gzhan du min// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// mdzad pa'i sna tshogs gdul don du// phyogs bcu'i zhing khams ma lus par// phyi nang gsang ba'i tshul dag gis// theg pa mchog tu yongs grags pa'i// rdo rje theg pa'i lam gyur 'di// rgyal ba rgya mtsho ma lus pa'i// thugs kyi snying po gsang ba yin// sku dang gsung gi rdo rje 'dir// snying po kun du 'dus pa'i phyir// rnal 'byor bas ni rtag tu spros// 'dir ni sngon chad bstan pa'ang med// ma 'ongs pa na'ang 'byung bar dka'// de bas gsang chen rnyed dka' bas// sangs rgyas rnams ni 'jig rten du// 'byung bar 'gyur ram ma byon yang // gsang ba'i yi ge rnam dag pa// 'phel 'grib spangs pas gnas pa yin// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i gnas// gsang chen rang 'byung mnyam pa nyid// dpal mchog 'di ni bsdus pa'i tshul// ye shes chen po'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la gsang ba 'jig rten du 'byung bar dka' bar gdams shing bstan pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba las sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mdzad pa bstan pa'i le'u ste nyer drug pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa srid mtha' gzigs sangs rgyas thams cad kyis srid pa'i chu klung skems pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'dir ni srid pa'i dra ba dag // rnam par gcod cing ye shes mes// sdug bsngal gnas 'di bsreg par bya// de nyid bde ba kun gyi gnas// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zla ba sgra gcan sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i ri bo 'joms par byed pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rtog pa sna tshogs las bcas pa// g.yeng bas sdug bsngal phung por gyur// de bsal ye shes byang chub sems// blang dor med pa'i ngang du gnas// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen zla ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi phyag rgya'i gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// kun du phyag rgyas rgyas btab pas// mi phyed ye shes bdag nyid gyur// de nyid phyag rgya bzhi ldan pas// thams cad sdom par snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du rtog las rnam byung ba/ de nyid 'joms pa'i rdo rje ni// stong nyid bde chen byang chub sems// de nyid ye shes tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gshegs pa mdzod spu ldan pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sangs rgyas kun gyi sdom pa ni// thabs dang shes rab dbyer med pa// dus gsum de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs// 'du 'bral med pa'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa spobs pa grags pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dngos grub gdul bya la ster bar mdzad pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'dir ni so so rang rig pa// ye shes rgyun chad med pa'i lam// de nyid lam du bsgom pa'i mchog // bsam gtan ye shes tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje nor bu sangs rgyas thams cad kyi na bza' mi zad pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// nor bu'i snying po bsam 'phel bzhin// rtog med bsam pa rdzogs byed pa// rang byung chos kyi sgra ston pas// mi gnas ye shes tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi khyu mchog rdo rje'i rtsal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// srid dang zhi bar mi gnas pa// rdo rje gsum mchog dam pa'i dbyings// sku gsum lam gyi ye shes bcas// sa gsum dag pa'i dbang phyug thob// ces gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa nor bu bkod pa'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rin po che sna tshogs pa'i mdangs bkod pa/ rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rjes su dran pa'i gnas ni mthong ba'i lam// ye shes skad cig dga' ba bcu drug las// phyi nang gnas pas 'od gsal don rtogs pa// stong nyid rang 'byung rnam dag tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dbang chen seng ge'i nga ro sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mchod pa'i rgya mtsho mchod pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sna tshogs snang ba du mar 'char ba nyid// yul ni sgyu ma dngos po gdod nas dag // dag pa'i ngo bo chos dbyings nam mkha' che// sems snang rol pa gsang ba 'dir bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan 'byung gnas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba rmad du byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// ma btsal ma spangs ngang gis dag pa'i sku// rnyed par mi 'gyur rab 'byam bde ba che// bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam ni lhun grub pa// byang chub sems chen gsang ba theg pa'i mchog // ces gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa lhun po grags sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba mtshan rab 'bar ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// bde bar gshegs pa'i mtshan dang dpe byad rnams// sems can kun gyi lus la nges par bzhugs// dbri bsnan med par 'char pas gsal bar byed// de nyid sbas pa'i don du tshul 'di bstan// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zer bcu pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po gzhal yas khang nye bar brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i gzhal yas khang // tshad med bkod pas rab spras pa// rgyan rnams bye brag mtha' yas tshogs// snang bde nyid tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ma dmad pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po yang dag par ston pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sgyu ma'i chos rnams mkha' lta bur// dag pa'i ye shes rang srog go// snying gi pad+ma sad par bya// de las ye shes blo rgyas pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de dag kun gyi gsang // ye shes dam pa mchog grub pa// gsang chen ye shes lam 'di yis// 'dod dang thar bar bsgrub pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba las gsang ba chen po'i ye shes kyi don gtan la phab pa'i le'u ste nyer bdun pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa glang po'i 'gros sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bla na med pa'i ye shes la dmigs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// ye shes mchog tu gsang ba gang // de nyid bsdus par gyur pa ste// rtog pa'i dra ba gcod mdzad yin// de nyid tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa yid 'thad dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od zer kun nas rgyas pa'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du sangs rgyas 'od zer snang bas khyab// de nyid 'dom gang 'od ni dpa' rlabs gnyis// gnyis med gcig tu dag pas dbu ma nyid// dbyer med ye shes tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen zla ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub kyi shing mchog la dmigs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rin chen brtan pa'i ljon pa'i shing // de nyid byang chub sems las byung // skyes pa sems bskyed rten gyur pas// rang byung tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zhi ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi nyan thos chen po rnams kyis dpag par dka' ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// zab pa shin tu zhi ba'i gnas// rdul med rnyog pa med pa'i thugs// bsam gtan rdo rje tshad med pas// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rab gsal rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi nyan thos dgra bcom pa chen po rnams kyis brtag par dka' ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gnas pa med pa'i gnas gyur pa// khyu mchog chen po byang chub sems// rang gzhan mi phyed mi dmigs pas// de nyid tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thub pa kha lo sgyur ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas rgyun du zhugs pa rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'khor ba'i rgyun 'di mya ngan 'das// de nyid spang du med pas na// ye shes shes rab rab gnas pas// dag pa tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dge ba'i dbang phyug sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes phyir mi 'ong ba rnams kyis rtogs par dka' ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang phyir ldog pa med pa'i sems// 'di ni ye shes chen po'i ngang // bla na med pa snying po'i sku// de bzhin nyid kyi tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gtsug na rin po che'i 'od sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lan cig phyir 'ong ba rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// khams gsum snang ba sems yin phyir// sems de stong nyid rgyu med pas// gang du dri med gzhan don 'byung // 'di ni tshul chen gsang ba yin// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thub pa snyems bral sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zag pa zad pa rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du zag med 'byung ba med// khams dang dbang po yul med par// shin tu dri med nam mkha' bzhin// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen snying po'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba rang rgyal ba thams cad kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du lus kyi kun du spyod pa yi// rdzu 'phrul snang ba bstan nas 'dul byed pa// rang 'byung bsam gtan thob ste ltos med pa// gsang ba 'dir gnas ye shes tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zla ba'i zhal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba tshangs pas dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// thog ma med cing mtha' med pas// srid rtser mi gnas dbang phyug che// dngos po med cing rtag pa che// de nyid tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med par grags pa'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas brgya byin gyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du ma 'khrug rtog pa med// ye shes rgyal ba kun gyi yul// gzugs sogs yul ni rtog tu med// thams cad dag pa'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zhi ba'i gzi brjid sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spyod yul lha drag pos dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// nyon mongs 'ching bdag pa yi// sred len rkyen gol log pas na// dmigs med ye shes gsang ba nyid// ye shes tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thub pa dga' ba'i tog sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba khyab 'jug gis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang nas gang du khyab bya ngo bos stong // thams cad bdag med stong pa zhi ba'i phyir// sems can khams med 'jug par mi gnas pas// ye shes chen po'i tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa sgra gcan lha'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes gsang ba lha ma yin rnams kyi dmigs su med pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du sa 'og sa steng dang // sa bla rnams su bstan pa yi// dngos grub bdud rtsi thob byed pas// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dpal na tshod bzang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes gsang ba klu rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes sku// dug med gdug pa rnam bral bas// skyon med gtsang ba'i rang bzhin can// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa lha dga'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa mngon par rol pa srin mo rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// bdag med mnyam pa nyid thob pas// grub pa med pa'i gnas la ni// 'chi med ye shes tshul mchog gis// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen phung po sangs rgyas thams cad kyis sbas pa ye shes nam mkha'i bu mo rnams kyis dmigs su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du mkha' la spyod 'gro ba'i// gya gyur spyod pa'i ye shes can// de nyid de zhes rnam brtags pas// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mdzes par gshegs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes gnod sbyin rnams kyis rtogs par dka' ba thams cad kyi gnas pa rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rin chen gter 'chang mdzod po che// nor gyi rgya mtsho mtha' yas pas// de nyid sa dbang bde gshegs rgyal// gsang ba dam pa bka' stsal pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i gnas pa'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyis sbas pa 'jig rten pa thams cad dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa thams cad kyi skye dgu'i chos las dben pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// skyes bu chen po thams cad kyi// ye shes gnas ni mnyam med pas// rang gzhan mi phyed byang chub che// sems dpa' tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// gang du 'gro la gnas gyur pa'i// gsang chen 'dir ni gnas gyur na// gang la'ang dri mar mi 'gyur zhing // dgag par bya ba ci yang med// las rnams thams cad byas kyang ni// rang byung skur ni rnam par grol// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba'i rgyud las dag pa'i skyes bu bstan pa'i le'u ste nyer brgyad pa'o// // de nas yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shin tu mthor gshegs sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi mchod rten 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dri med ye shes dag pa'i gnas// rin chen phung po gsal ba yi// dang zhing yid 'phrog 'byung ba'i gzhi// sa le sgrib med tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par skye ba'i dbang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rdo rje mngon par 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// mngon par 'byung ba 'phags pa'i lam// nyes pa spongs pa'i tshul mchog gis// rnam par mthor gshegs 'og min te// zab pa brjod med tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa blo gros bzang po mthong ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rgyal ba'i gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dngos po kun gyi rang bzhin mchog // chos kun mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// kun mkhyen kun 'gro thams cad pa// dri med tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dpal 'jig rten 'od sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid gnas pa gcig pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos rnams kun gyi rang bzhin 'dzin// mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa po// mnyam nyid 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen gzi brjid sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kun rtog pa med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gcig dang du ma'i rang bzhin gnas// cher mi g.yo ba rang bzhin med// rtsol med 'byung bdag pa yi// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa skal ldan shing rta chen po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dpe byad las 'das pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// bcom ldan so so rang rig pa// gtso bo dpe bral ye shes te// bdag po kun 'gro kun khyab pas// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa kun du rgyal ba bzang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dngos po mi dmigs pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'byung gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// byed pa po dang 'phrog pa rang med/ 'di ni dpal ldan rang byung sems// dngos po gsal dang mi gsal mdzad// ye shes snang ba'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// bsgom du med// gang du ro mnyam mchog gi dngos/ byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa spos kyi glang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mi gnas pa rdo rje zhes bya bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa blo gros 'od 'phro'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes blo gros mi zad pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// shes rab mkha' la rnam par gnas/ snying rjes sad pa'i mda' yis ni/ bde ba chen po'i rnam par 'bigs/ byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de grol mtha' la mi gnas pa'o// dgos pa kun gyi 'ching ba bral/ byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen spos sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyi rdo rje mi zad pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gnyis med bde ba mchog tu zhi/ mkha' mnyam rtog pa las grol ba/ gnyis med rnam dag chos kyi dbyings/ byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa chos bstan sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbyings rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gnas pa che/ brtan g.yo dag pa'i tshul mchog gis/ dbyer med tshul 'di dag pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gzi brjid drag shul can sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bdud dpung thams cad pham par mdzad pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rtog pa ngan pas brtags pa yi/ phyi rol yul ni rdzas stong pas/ thabs dang shes rab rnam dag nyid/ ye shes tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi nor bu sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes dra ba gcod pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// bde ba chen po gcig nyid kyi/ nang du snod bcud dngos po'i chos/ kun rdzob bden pas stong ba'i phyir/ 'dus pa der gnas tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa bzang pos byin bas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i 'dam rdzab skems par byed pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du gnyis med ngang gnas pa// rang bzhin brtag tshogs rab zhi bas// snang gsum ye shes dag gyur ba'i// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zla ba'i bla ma sangs rgyas srid pa'i tshang tshing 'joms pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// phyi rol nga rgyal log bcom ste// ye shes gcig pu bdag dag pas// rang byung bsam pa rnam par dag // byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa tshangs pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas thams cad kyis log rtog 'joms pa'i ri bo rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// kun tu rtog pa rab spangs nas// 'dod chags chags bral ye shes las// dbu mar dmigs par mi 'gyur te// gsang ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i zla ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'byung gnas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rang rig nas ni byang chub 'gyur// 'dir nyid tha dad rtog min zhing // gzugs dang rnam thar sgo thim pas// chos rgyun thob phyir bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// 'gro ba rnams kyi bde ba rtags dang bcas 'byung ba// gang yin mtshan ma spangs par gyur pa'i phyir// rang byung ngo bo ye shes bdag nyid de// rtogs pas stong pa'i bde ba mi zad yin// rlung gi rtog pa'i rjes su 'jug pa ni// bde ba rang sems ngo bo dam pas ni// tshim 'gyur de las gzhan du g.yo mi 'gyur// thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid gnas pa yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis dam pa'i mdzod chen po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la bstan pa'i don to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba las/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bde ba mi 'gyur ba'i don bstan pa'i le'u ste nyer dgu pa'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mtshungs pa med pa'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po gsang ba dri ma med pa rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad rjes su dran pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te// byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// de bzhin gshegs kun 'dus pa yi// sangs rgyas spro bsdu'i 'khor lo yis// rtse mor gyur pa'i phyag rgya yis// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa legs par skyes pa'i dpal sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes gsang ba chos rdo rje rjes su dran pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// rang byung ye shes zhi ba'i dngos// dag pa rnam dben mngon par 'byung // phun sum tshogs pa lam gyur gnas// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thub pa dpe med pa'i tshogs sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba rigs rdo rje rjes su dran pa zhes bya ba'i ting ge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gang du lha dang lha mo dang // byang chub sems dpa' dpag med pa// ye shes las skyes mtshungs med pa// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa grags pa'i bshes gnyen sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdo rje'i rigs rjes su dran pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// gdug pa can rnams gdul bya'i phyir// snying rjes gtum pa'i nga ro yis// tshar gcad pa nyid bla med bsgral// de nyid gsang ba'i tshul bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa bden pa'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rdo rje rjes su dran pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge la 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// lha dang lha min lto 'phye dang / grul bu ma la sogs sna tshogs pas// bstod cing mchod pa'i ye shes gnas// rin chen 'khor lo brjod pa yin/ zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dka' thub chen po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rin po che'i nor bu rjes su dran pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// de nas ye shes nor dbugs drug gis ni dbyug gu phyed// dbyug gu gnyis la chu tshod gcig // chu tshod sum cu rtsa gnyis las// thun ni rnam pa brgyad du phri// 'pho ba'i tshul ni bcu drug go// dbyug gu dag pa'i gnas yin pas// drug cu rtsa bzhir gnas pa'o// spyir na sems can khams la ni// rtog pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa// de snyed yod phyir shes pa des// rlung yang bsam gyis mi khyab po// de yang bsdus pa'i don du ni// nyon mongs brgyad khri bzhi stod pas// rnam par dbye ba mkhas pa yis// zag bcas rlung ni ri phrag brgyad// lhag pa stong phrag bzhi las ni// zag pa med pa'i rlung gyur pa// khri phrag gnyis kyis dag pa yin// rlung rags pas ni rtog pa'i tshogs// de dang mtshungs par 'jug pa yin// rtog pa bka' nyal gyur bas// rlung ni phra bar gyur pa ste// phrag rags rtog pa dag bas ni// rlung ni shin tu phra bar 'gyur// rnam rtog dang ni rlung gnyis gang // mtshungs par mnyam par 'byung 'jug las// rlung gi 'jug pa 'byung med par// rtog pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur bas// de phyir las kyi rlung dag ni// khri phrag gnyis dang stong dag dang // drug brgya dag tu shes par bya// yi ge'i dbye ba'i gnas kyis ni// rang bzhin mngon par 'byung ba yin// yi ge dang ni rang bzhin gnyis// gnas dang rten du shes par bya// yi ge dag pas rtog pa dag// rtog pa 'od gsal gnas su spyod// yi ge rnam pa lus gnas pas// drug gsum rang bzhin rgya drug cu// nyin mtshan sbyor bas 'byung bas na// lus gnas yi ge brgya dang ni// drug cu gnas las 'byung zhing 'jug // de phyir gsang ba'i yi ge yis// thams cad za zhing lding bar 'gyur// gnam mkha' mtha' med rtag pa'i don// sems can kun gyi gnas chen po// dpal gyis 'byor pa bla med rgyal// bsam pa thams cad rdzogs byed pa'o// A li bcu drug phrag gnyis las// zhe sdang las gyur rtog pa 'byung // de yi rtsa ba thig ler bcas// sum cu gsum du gyur pa yin// kA li sum cu rtsa bzhi dang // ya ra la wa dad+ha ste// bzhi bcu mngon par gnas pas na// 'dod chags rtog pa de snyed yin// zung gyur drug ldan thig ler bcas// mtshan ma bdun gyis mtshon pa'i phyir// dbus ma la brten gti mug pa'i// rang bzhin mi rig gyur pa'o// snga ma g.yas rtsa la brten pa// skyes pa rdo rjer bcas gyur brjod// gong du g.yon rtsa las 'byung ba// bud med pad+ma'i mtshan mas brjod// rtsa yi byed ba mi 'dra ste// khams dang rnam shes 'du ba yi// rten du gyur phyir rtsa yin te// rnam par bzlog na gnyis su 'gyur// thig le 'pho 'gyur phyi rol bzhin// zla ba lus la 'pho ba ste// tshes gcig la sogs rkang g.yon nas// mthe bo sogs 'phel spyi bor gnas// de nas g.yas kyi cha la ni// zla ba rim gyis 'grib par 'gyur// 'phel dang 'grib pa'i khyad par gyis// lnga byang chub sems skyed byed// dkar phyogs nag po ri ma shes bya// spyod pa'i tshul ni de bder spyad// gnam stod nyi ma gsang bar te// zla ba nya gang tshes gcig rgyas// khyad par sgra gcan rim shes bya// bla na med pa rags pa dang phra ba'i gnas 'jug ldog bstan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// de nas gsang ba rab tu 'dzin pa pos// khyad par sems gsum rim pa bka' stsal te// snang ba zhes bya rnam par mi rtog pa// gsal ba'i cha ste gzung rtog spangs pa las// 'byung ba mi mngon rlung dang bcas pa gang // lhang nger gnas pa skad cig dang po yin// mched pa'i snang ba rab tu mi rtog ste// ches gsal ba las 'dzin rtog ma zhugs pa// ye shes phra ba rlung ldan mi snang ba// lhan ne gnas pa skad cig gnyis pa yin// thob pa'i cha ni shin tu mi rtog pa// gsal ba tsam du 'ang mi gnas shin tu phra// rlung sems mi phyed gsal bar 'char ba min// lham me gnas pa skad cig gsum pa yin// nye bar thob pa dri ma med pa ste// rang byung rang gsal bde ba dmigs su med/ phra rags rab gsal ting nge 'dzin du gnas// skad cig bzhi pa mi 'gyur khyab byed yin// 'od gsal ba ni gsam gtan zag pa med// rdul med sa bon med pas mi g.yo ba// lhan cig gnas pa chos sku'i snying po ni// lhun grub byang chub sems kyi ngo bo nyid// sgyu ma 'di nyid yod med las 'das shing // dbu ma tsam du'ang mi gnas kun rdzob ste// chos rnams thams cad sgyu ma'i snang ba las// 'gas pa med pa'i rol par rang byung ba'o// zung 'jug bde ba chen po'i mtshan nyid can// chos dbyings chos nyid dbyer med dag pa'i sku// tha dad rnam bral mi phyed ye shes te// gsang ba chen po'i lam las 'dir rtogs bya// thun mong dbang phyug dang ni rtags bcas pa// dbang phyug brgyad ldan 'char ba 'di nyid do// phra zhing yang la phra bar nub pa dang // spyod par nus dang bdag nyid chen po dang // dga' mgur byed cing thams cad dbang du 'gyur// ci 'dod byed dang dbang phyug don du 'char// sku yi dbang phyug gsung gi dbang phyug dang // thugs kyi dbang phyug de nyid phrin las dang // rdzu 'phrul kun du 'gro ba'i dbang phyug dang // gang 'dod bskyed dang khyad bar don brgyad do// phung po khams dang skye mched bsdus pa yi// lnga po'i dbye ba lnga ru byas pa la// de bzhin gshegs pa so sor byin gyis rlabs// 'khor ba'i las rnams dag ni rnam dag pas// de bzhin dbang po'i phyi rol yul bcas lda// re re zhing yang bde gshegs lda rnams kyi// de la rang rang rtag tu byin gyis rlob// ye shes lnga dang gsum du gnas pas yang dag bsdus// zhes gsungs te// gsang ba zab pa'i tshul bstan pa rdo mi phyed pa'i ye shes kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang // gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa ba'o// de nas bcom ldan bde gshegs kun// gsang chen ye shes rdo rje 'dzin// sems can don du yang dag 'byung // blo ldan byang chub sems dpa' yis// don kun thub pa rdo rje 'dzin// rgyal ba de la btud byas te// gsang ba dam tshig mkhyen pa la// mchod cing bstod pas gsang chen gyi// rdo rje dbyangs ni bshad pa yin// e ma tshul bzang sangs rgyas pa// de nyid rigs brgya bsdus pa'i sku// de nyid tshul 'di gsungs so// lta ba ma yin mi gnas pa// kun gzhi dag pa'i snying po nyid// zab cing phra ba rten gyur pas// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gzugs mchog rgyal bo sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// 'khor 'das gzung 'dzin snod bcud rnams// byang chub dam pa'i gzhi// byang chub sems zhes brjod pa yin// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid tshangs dbyangs rdo rje'i nga ro yis// chos 'byung rol ba ston par mdzad// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skar mkhan thams cad kyi bdag rnam par dag pa rdo ba don spyod pa'o// zhes gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zla ba'i sgron me 'bar ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsob po rnam par dag pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te thob la// des chos thams cad yongs su dag cing phyin ci ma log par khong du chud pas gnas par byed do// 'jig rten gyi lha chen po tshangs pa dang / brgya byin dang / khyab 'jug dang / dbang phyug chen
