dang shes rab 'khor lo'i gtso// dngos grub 'dis ni bsdus pa yin// zhes bka' stsal to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor dpag tu med pa rnams kyi ched du brjod pa yang dag par bstan pa/ gang du yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba ma lus pa snying po gcig tu yang dag par gsungs pa ste// 'di ni bsod nams thams cad kyi 'byung gnas// phun sum tshogs pa'i khyad par yid bzhin gyi nor bu chos bla na med pa gsang chen rdo rje'i theg pa// phyir rgol ba thams cad kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba mi 'phrog pa// sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa yang dag bar rdzogs par byed pa/ lam thams cad kyi rgyal po las/ bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis thub pa med cing zil gyis mi non pa bdud kyi rigs ma lus pa'i gnas kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu 'joms par byed pa/ kun du rgyu ba'i log sred can rnams kyis glags rnyed par mi 'gyur ba'i yul tha snyad thams cad las rnam par 'das pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i mtshungs pa med cing kun las gol ba'i don te/ gsang ba chen po'i tshul 'di bstan pa'i tshe// spyod pa bla na med pa 'di thos pa'o// lha dang mi dang lha min dbang po dang // tshangs brtsegs rnam grol 'bras bu rab tu thob// gtsang ma lha rnams bya ba rab tu dga'// dbang po tshangs pa bar snang mkha' la gnas// bde bar gshegs la shin tu mchod par byas// byang chub sems dpa' bye ba mtha' yas pa// bar snang gnas te rab tu dga' gyur cing // chu yi sprin med yid du 'ong ba dag // 'gro ba'i dug sel dri zhim bdug par byed// lha yi dbang po rab bsgyur rab dang zhi// mkha' las lha 'khor khrag khrig dpag med dang // rim gror bcas pas gos rnams 'thor bar byed// yid 'ong gos brgya dag gis gtor bar gyur// 'dod par spyod pa'i lha yi bu mo dag // ri rab sum cu rtsa drug rdul phran gyi// grangs mnyam dag gis dgyes pa'i rol mos mchod// gzugs la spyod pa'i lha yi bu mang po// ri rab sum cu rtsa drug rdul mnyam pas// kun nas de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod de// rol mo brdung ba bye ba khrag khrig dag // rig pa 'dzin pa'i 'khor lo dpag tu med// de snyed gsang ba 'dzin pa'i rjes 'brang zhing // byang chub sems dpa' rnam par 'phrul pa ston// e ma sgra dbyangs yan lag kun 'byung ba// kun du bzang po'i rnam 'phrul du mar shar// zhing mchog gcig na bde gshegs bzhugs mdzad pa// zhing rnams du mar sku gzugs rab tu bstan// de nyid sangs rgyas stong phrag gcig nyid las// sangs rgyas bye phrag stong ni gong du bstan// gsung gcig gis ni rab tu gang bstan pa// bsam yas gang gA'i klung gi bye snyed du// tshul rnams mi zad chos sgra sgrogs par mdzad// de snyed gsang ba mchog 'di rgyas par bkang // gang du ye shes rdo rje mi 'byung ba'i// ting 'dzin gcig pa nges par bzhugs nas ni// chos kyi dbyings las 'byung ba du ma yi// ting 'dzin sgo ni nam mkha' khyab par 'byung // sangs rgyas skus ni zhing khams khrag khrig dag // yid 'ong sna tshogs khyab pa'i ye shes sku// chos dbyings rgya chen yongs su rgyas bar bkang // ba spu gcig las bde ldan 'od bkye ba// 'gro ba'i nyon mongs yid 'ong zhi bar spro// zhing gi rdul phran zad par nus 'gyur gyi// 'di dag bgrang bar shes par mi nus so// 'khor los sgyur ba'i dam par la las mthong // la las sangs rgyas mtshan rab mnga' bar mthong // la las rigs drug thub pa sprul par mthong // zhing rnams la lar spyod pa mchog mdzad cing // dag cing rkang gnyis zhi ba dam pa mthong // dga' ldan gnas na mgon po bzhugs pa dang // rgyal tshab bsko mdzad nye bar 'pho ba bstan// gshegs dang gzigs pa de dag rab tu bstan// zhing rnams bye bar yum gyi lhums 'jug dang // zhing rnams kun du skye ba ston pa nyid// gzhon nu rol cing sgyu rtsal gnas pas mkhas// pho brang btsun mo'i nang na bzhugs par ston// 'gro ba'i don du mgon po nges 'byung zhing // dka' thub spyad cing de las ldang bar ston// mi g.yo go 'phang du ni gnas byas shing // bsam gtan bskul ba mdzad dang rgyal ba thob// rgyal ba'i dus las bslang ba 'di dag gis// gsang ba mngon par byang chub de nyid bstan// byang chub snying po rdo rje gdan du gshegs// de nyid bcom ldan mngon par sangs rgyas la// sa yi lha mo dgyes pas khyab byas shing // bdud sde bcom pas mi 'gyur mchog gi gnas// gsang ba 'og min 'di ni ye shes yul// gnyis med rdo rje'i gnas su rdzogs sangs rgyas// chos kyi 'khor lo des legs lam bstan pa// mtshan nyid med pa'i tshul du gsang ba bstan// rgyud sde yan lag phyi nang gsang ba yi// rnam pa gsum du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor// de ltar de bzhin gshegs pas tshul 'di gsungs// stong pa zhi ba bdag med mtshan nyid bral// chos nyid rang byung mkha' dang mtshungs pa las// rgyal bas don dam rab tu mi gnas pa// chos nyid stong nyid de bzhin nyid du ni// rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i chos rnams la// rgyu rkyen 'bras bus grub pa yang dag lam// kun rdzob spyod yul yin par rab tu bstan// zhing mang mtha' yas kun du de nyid ston// sgyu ma'i mkhan po mkhas pas gang du ni// 'gro ba'i gzugs brnyan du ma ston pa bzhin// de bzhin ston pa ye shes mchog mkhyen pa// kun du 'gro ba'i don du rab tu ston// thams cad ma lus chos nyid de 'dra ste// mtshan dang mtshan gzhi mnyam pa nyid kyis 'dra// mtshan nyid med pa chos rnams kun gyi mchog // bde bar gshegs pa'i lam 'di thob 'dod pas// rtog dang rnam rtog ma lus spang med pas// gsang chen tshul 'di gang gis spyod pa ni// dngos dang dngos med mnyam nyid shes par gyis// gang du rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug du ma'i spyod yul gsang ba chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ting nge 'dzin mtshungs pa med par spyod pa 'di la 'di lta ste/ gsang ba chen po bla na med pa'i tshul 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis chos thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa rab tu spyod pa// gsang ba chen po chos kyi tshul/ chos kyi dbyings lta ba po med pa/ chos thams cad shes pa po med par yang dag par ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa nyid du yang dag par lta ste/ ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob pas chos thams cad la lus med par rab tu mthong ba/ chos nyid de bzhin nyid kyi rgya mtsho la mi gnas pa'i tshul bstan pa nyid do// srid pa dang zhi ba'i chos thams cad rab tu zhi ba nyid nam mkha' lta bur gnas pa/ 'dus byas kyi khams 'dus ma byas su mngon par spags par mi byed la/ 'dus ma byas kyi khams 'dus byas su sgro btags pa thams cad kyis rnam par mi rtog par gnas pa ste/ 'di nyid sangs rgyas rnams kyis byin brlabs pa// bsod nams yongs su rgyas pa dag pa'i zhing // snang ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa'i 'od zer ni// skye dgu kun gyi blo yi 'char byed pa// gang du sku gsung thugs kyi snang ba ni// rnam par gsal ba sgrib pa med pa nyid// chos rnams kun la yang dag rab 'jug cing // chos kyi dbyings las ye shes 'bral med pa// lus ngag yid gnas kun gyi rjes 'gro ba'i// skad cig nyid la bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// skad cig thog mtha' med par rab ston pa// 'di ni ye shes mi zad 'byung gnas kyi// tshul la gnas pa gsag ba'i spyod tshul lo// brtan pas kun du rtog pa rab zhi ba// 'di ni mi gnas gsang ba'i spyod yul 'thob// sems can rgyud na'ang mi spyod ma yin te// 'di 'dra'i ye shes dam pa khong du chud// de la kun du rtog dang mi rtog med// blo mchog de dang 'gro kun kha lo sgyur// rnam par smin pas gos med nam mkha' bzhin// 'jig rten thams cad rgyu dang bcas pas na// chos rnams kun du rgyu med bstan pa min// 'di nyid rab dang 'bring dang tha ma yi// phyogs bcur ye shes bzhugs pa'i byang chub tshul// gsang ba dam pa'i spyod yul 'di bstan pa'o// chos thams cad kyi gnas ye shes kyi yul sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rab 'byam tshad med pa'i rdo rje btsun mo'i b+ha ga las mngon par 'byung ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i snying po'i dkyil 'khor las/ yang dag pa'i thugs rje chen po'i ngang las ye shes kyi sprin rdo rjes kun du khyab par spro ba dang sdud pa'i tshul gyis gang du mi gnas shing rang 'byung chen po'i byang chub kyi sems rdo rje/ chos kyi dbyings nam mkha' dang mnyam pa dbyings dang ye shes dbyer med par ngo bo nyid dmigs su med pa nyid du ston to// de nas dpal rdo rje 'dzin pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'gyur ba med pa'i ngo bo nyid rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems kyi gsang ba mi zad pa'i tshul 'di gsungs so// gsang ba spros med 'gyur ba med pa'i ngang // kun du ma skyes skye med dga' ba'i dbyings// bde chen ro mnyam rgyal ba kun gyi gnas// chos kun rang bzhin yongs su mnyam pa nyid// mngon par chags med mi gnas ye shes las// rlom sems med pa'i chos nyid skye ba med// ye shes chos kyi sgo yi ting nge 'dzin// nam mkha'i chos nyid 'byam klas thogs med pa// byang chub sems ldan bde gshegs spyod yul can// rdo rje lta bu'i gnas las bstan pa dang // phyir mi ldog pa ye shes 'byung gnas nyid// thams cad mkhyen pa tshad med 'bras bu'i yul// grangs med gzhal du med pa'i don 'byung ba'o// 'di dag kyang ji ltar rtogs par bya ba yin zhe na/ rnam par 'phrul pa'i sa khong du chud pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rjes su song zhing rjes su chags pa med par spyod pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi tshul la chos su rtogs pas gnas pa med pa sems bskyed pa shin tu yangs pas rnam par thar pa'i sgo du mar rab tu thob pa/ ye shes gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rgyud la mkhas pa/ don gcig nas gcig tu bstan pa rab tu 'jug pa bla na med pa'i ye shes dam pa'i spyod yul yin par rig par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gsang ba chen po'i rgyud 'dir gsang ba'i yi ge de dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i dam tshig gi spyod pa'i rdo rje 'di la dad cing bsgom par 'gyur/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin pas de dag la 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gsang ba'i yi ge gsum dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi gsang chen gyi spyod pa rdo rje gang yin pa 'di la dad cing bsgom par 'gyur ro// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol pa/ gsang ba'i yi ge gang zhig lags/ dpal rdo rje 'dzin pas bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i gsang ba chen po'i rdo rje dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi gsang ba chen po'i rdo rje dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi gsang ba chen po'i rdo rje ste/ de dag nyid do// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje 'dzin pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dud nas cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// kun mchog ye shes ston mdzad pas// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// gsang ba dam pa bka' stsal to// sangs rgyas kun gyis mi gsungs shing // don chen 'bras bu lam gyur pa// de bzhin gshegs pa gsang ba'i rgyud// rdo rje 'chang gis sbas pa nyid// u dum bA ra'i me tog bzhin// 'jig rten du ni rnyed dka' ba// kun gyi rtsa bar gyur pa'i mdo// gsang ba 'dus pa chen po yin// dbyings gyur khams gsum gsang ba che// de nyid bde bar 'gyur bsams pa// rdo rje gsum gyi gnas mtshan pas// ting 'dzin rdo rje khyu mchog dgyes// thabs dang shes rab dbyer med pa// 'di ni gang zhig gnas byed pa// byang chub sems dpa'i grags chen rnams// zhag bdun gyis ni phun tshogs pa'i// sku gsum dngos grub 'dir thob 'gyur// bcom ldan sku gsung thugs gsang ba// rdo rje bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor la// dri med ye shes 'byung ba yi// khyad par mchog 'di phyung ba'o// sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig ni// phyag rgya chen po'i don rtogs pa// cho ga bzhin du kun bsgoms na// skad cig gis ni sangs rgyas 'thob// gsang ba'i don 'di 'byung dka' ba'i// bla med bde chen mi 'gyur ba// 'di ni snying po bsdus pa ste// gzhan du 'byung bar 'gyur ba min// 'on kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba 'dus pa chen po 'di la skad cig thang cig yud tsam gyis gnas na sangs rgyas kyi byang chub rdzogs par byed do// bskal pa gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed thams cad du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis 'bad cing rtsol kyang byang chub thob par mi 'gyur ba de dpal gsang ba 'dus ba la dga' ba'i byang chub sems dpas tshe 'di nyid la de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o// de dag shin tu dkon gyur pa// rnam grangs 'di na bstan pa'i tshe// de tshe byang chub sems dpa' rnams// shin tu gdung bas cher non te// gsang chen bskal pa ngan gyur ces// dus gcig bstan pa nyid gcig dang // ston pa gcig las gzhan pa yi// spyod yul ma gyur de yi tshe// ji ltar thabs 'di ston byed 'gyur// ming tsam du yang mi thos na// gzhan ci smos lta ga la dgos// de nyid kun du bsgrags gyur pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ de skad ces ma zer cig // yi ge 'di kun dang thun mong ste// rigs kyi bu khyed rnams kyis ji ltar mi shes pa dang / ma thob pa de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad kyi gsang ba'i yi ge 'di dag ma thob cing mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// de ci'i phyir zhe na// gsang ba'i yi ge ni rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad cang mi smra bar gnas par gyur to// de nas rdo rje 'dzin pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos gsang ba'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po mnyam pa nyid la rnam par dgongs nas cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas yang brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos 'di ci'i slad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang // byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi nang na cang mi gsung bar bzhugs// de skad ces gsol pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bdag po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po 'di ci'i slang du sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ngo bo nyid las dmigs su med pa'i yi ge'i tshogs la ngo bo nyid med pa'i yi ge'i tshig brjod nas cang mi gsung bar bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po rdo rje btsun mo'i b+ha ga la snyoms par zhugs so// de nas lha mo bzhi dag gis// tshad med ye shes dag pa'i sa// yang dag bskul ba mdzad pa las// de bzhin nyid las bzhengs par 'gyur// dpag med rdo rje'i tshul mchog las// 'dod chags gnas la spyod pa yi// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs na// btsun mo'i tshogs dang lhan cig skyes// dam tshig 'khor lor gnas pa yis// 'dod pa'i longs spyod nyer ldan pas// gnyis med byang chub sems gnas te// dgyes pa yongs su spyod pa mdzad// de nas rdo rje'i lus kyi ni// rtsa yi khog stong thams cad du// bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje dang // yon tan phrin las dam tshig gi// khu ba byang chub sems rgyun gyis// kun tu khyab par gyur pa ni// dper na bum pa chus gang ltar// shin tu bde bas rgyas par gnas// de nyid ye shes gyur pa'o// de nas chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i// 'gro ba'i phung po ji snyed kun// sku gsum dam tshig las byung ba// de la bdud rtsi'i 'od zer gyis// glog gi zer ma ltar 'phro bas// shin tu bde bar rig nas ni// de nas brtsams te sems can khams// ma lus lus pa med pa la// rdo rje dpal gyi reg byung bas// yang dag mchog tu byin brlabs shing // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yis// ye shes dri med dbang bskur cing // ma lus kun kyang kun tu bzang // kun tu bzang po'i dpal zhes par// bla na med par dbang bskur to// de ltar dbang bskur tsam gyis ni// thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku// dgra bcom yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas// rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes can// bde chen ngo bo nyid skur gyur// rdo rje 'dzin gyis bka' stsal pa// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ye shes spyod pa mthong gyur pas// chos nyid mnyam pa nyid mthong ngam// slar gsol ba ni mthong lags so// ye shes spyod pa rdo rje che// bde bar gshes pa mthong zhes gsol// de ltar yang dag gyur pa'o// de ltar sangs rgyas thams cad kun// rdo rje btsun mo'i b+ha ga las// mngon par byung nas 'di skad gsol// gang du 'dod chags chen po yi// yi ge'i tshogs kyis sangs rgyas kyi// byang chub rjes su rtogs gyur gang // de nas bcom ldan ngo mtshar to// bde bar gshegs pa ngo mtshar to// de nas rigs kyi bdag po yis// gsang ba mchog tu bka' stsal pa// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' kun// de skad ces ni ma zer cig // de nyid ci yi phyir zhe na// chos rnams nam mkha'i rdo rje'i gnas// de nyid mtshungs phyir stong pa nyid// rab tu mi gnas bdag nyid las// chos rnams 'od gsal dbyings gyur pa// de nyid ye shes 'byung gnas gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'i mnyams pa nyid spyod pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// snyoms par zhugs nas kyang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang / rig ma dang / lha mo dang / khro bo'i rgyal po du ma dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo la bzhugs nas cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje 'dzin pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad la bka' stsal pa/ khyed rnams kyis phyogs bcu mtha' yas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gsang ba 'di bgo bar gyis shig // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ phyogs bcu na gnas pa ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de rnams chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la skal ba yod pa'i phyir ro// gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying po la bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i dam tshig rdo rje 'di nyid zung cig // khyod kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje snying po dbang phyug gsang ba'i rgyal po zhes bya bar dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos de bzhin du bgyi'o// zhes gsol nas/ cang mi smra bar gyur to// gsang ba'i rgyal po'i sku gcig las// zhing khams ma lus snang mdzad cing // khams gsum spyod dang sangs rgyas gyi// rnam pa du ma'i skur bstan mdzad// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad khams gsum nyid kyi lus rdo rje la gnas shing // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i ye shes mnyam pa nyid la dgongs nas/ cang mi gsung bar gyur to// gsang ba 'dzin pa'i gsung gcig gis// 'jig rten khams kun khyab gyur cing // chos kyi tshul ni mi zad las// rgyun mi 'chad pa'i 'khor lo bskor// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gsung rdo rje 'di dpag tu med pa khams gsum pa thams cad kyi ngag rdo rje la gnas shing // de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung mnyam pa nyid la gnas nas/ cang mi gsung bar gyur to// rdo rje 'chang gi thugs kyi ni// ting 'dzin gcig tu ma bzhag nas// ting 'dzin du ma'i chos kyi sgo// chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam par 'gyur// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje 'dzin pa'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sems rdo rje la gnas shing // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs mnyam pa nyid la dmigs nas/ cang mi gsung bar gyur to// 'dir snang ba ni gsum ste// so so'i skye bo'i snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i snang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i snang ba'o// gsang ba ni gsum ste// sku'i gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang // gsung gi gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang // thugs kyi gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// thams cad mkhyen pa ni gsum ste/ sku rdo rje thams cad mkhyen pa dang / gsung rdo rje thams cad mkhyen pa dang / thugs rdo rje thams cad mkhyen pa'o// mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo ni gsum ste/ sku mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo dang / gsung mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo dang / thugs mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo nyid do// rgyud kun snying po bsdus pa yi// phyag rgya chen po'i ngang 'byung ba// grub pa rab tu mi gnas pas// gsang ba'i rgyal po bstan pa yin// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa chen po bla na med pa mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i gnas rab tu rgyas pa chen po bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ gsang ba brjod du med pa'i gnas la dgongs nas/ cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs dpag tu med pa de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brjod du med pa'i tshogs dang bcas pa thams cad dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// // dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa phyogs bcu'i gnas kyi zhing khams rdul phra rab snyed bzhugs shing 'tsho skyong ba thams cad kyi gsang chen/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po la sogs pa/ bskal pa gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod kyis mi lang ba rnams kyi dgongs pa rab tu gsang ba/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad kyi/ shin tu gsang ba'i gnas kyi rgyal po/ rdo rje dpal mchog chen po nges par brjod pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i ye shes kyi 'byung gnas// rnal 'byor chen po gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid/ rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba mchog tu dbang skur bar byed pa/ rgyud sde stong phrag sum cu rtsa bzhi'i snying po/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod rgya mtsho'i gnas las mngon par bsngags pa/ rtog pa'i rgyal po bdun pa chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i don bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun cu rtsa bdun pa'o// // du la k+She tra'i grong khyer chen por rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ye shes snying po dang / bod kyi lo ts+tsha ba mar pa lho brag pa chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa// // paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po smr-i ti dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur byas pa cig kyang yod par gda'o// // e ma ho nyi zla ltar grags dpal ldan 'dus pa'i rgyud// gsang ba rnal 'byor dpal mchog chen po 'dis// shin tu gsal bar ston pa nges pa nyid// ma 'ongs dus su rnal 'byor dbang phyug mchog // rnam bzhi'i 'khor ldan dbus su 'di gsal 'gyur// bstan pa'i sgron me nyid du 'byung ba'i phyir// skal ldan rnams dang rgyud 'di 'phrad par shog // rgyud 'di u rgyan nas slob dpon chen po Dom bi he ru kas gdan drangs gsung ngo rdzogs so//
